#Inauguration Speech
country_event = {
	id = LBJ.1
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event LBJ.1" }
	title = LBJ.1.t
	desc = LBJ.1.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_rally

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = LBJ.1.a
		add_political_power = 50
		add_stability = 0.05
	}
}

	}

#Determine how strong the Voting Rights Act will be
country_event = {
	id = LBJ.13
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event LBJ.13" }
	title = LBJ.13.t
	desc = LBJ.13.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_congress_2

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { #strengthen bill
		name = LBJ.13.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = USA_LBJ_CIVIL_RIGHTS option = USA_LBJ_CIVIL_RIGHTS_MODERATE }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = USA_LBJ_CIVIL_RIGHTS option = USA_LBJ_CIVIL_RIGHTS_WEAK }
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -100
		hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = LBJ_VRA_strong }
	}
	option = { #keep it as is
		name = LBJ.13.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = USA_LBJ_CIVIL_RIGHTS option = USA_LBJ_CIVIL_RIGHTS_STRONG }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = USA_LBJ_CIVIL_RIGHTS option = USA_LBJ_CIVIL_RIGHTS_WEAK }
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -50
		hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = LBJ_VRA_medium }
	}
	option = { #weaken it
		name = LBJ.13.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = USA_LBJ_CIVIL_RIGHTS option = USA_LBJ_CIVIL_RIGHTS_STRONG }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = USA_LBJ_CIVIL_RIGHTS option = USA_LBJ_CIVIL_RIGHTS_MODERATE }
			}
		}
		add_political_power = 50
		hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = LBJ_VRA_weak }
	}
}

	desc = hart.100.desc

	hidden = yes

	option = { #
		name = hart.100.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
		add_to_variable = { USA_BOSTON_NYC_PROGRESS = 10 }
		clamp_variable = { var = USA_BOSTON_NYC_PROGRESS max = 100 }
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { USA_BOSTON_NYC_PROGRESS < 100 } }
			country_event = { id = hart.100 days = 15 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { USA_BOSTON_NYC_PROGRESS = 100 } }
			USA_HART_increase_transportation_reform = yes
		}
	}
}

	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event hart.senate.35" }
	title = hart.senate.35.t
	desc = hart.senate.35.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_rally

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			USA_reset_stockpile_support = yes
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = hart.senate.35.a
		TNO_improve_admin_efficiency_high = yes
		TNO_worsen_education_policy_effectiveness_monthly_high = yes

		set_temp_variable = { USA_temp_upkeep_cost_var = 0.01 }
		USA_upkeep_cost_adjust = yes
		set_temp_variable = { USA_temp_equality_var = 0.04 }
		USA_equality_adjust = yes
		set_temp_variable = { USA_temp_happiness_var = -0.02 }
		USA_happiness_adjust = yes

		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_cram_school_unlocked_tt
		set_country_flag = USA_unlocked_Cram_School
	}
}

					var = USA_crime_bill_harsh

					compare = greater_than
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = USA_weakish_cb

			custom_effect_tooltip = USA_urban_voters_header_tt

			set_temp_variable = { USA_week_change_urban_rep = 4 }
			add_to_variable = { Demographic_Shift_urban_rep_Weeks = USA_week_change_urban_rep }
			add_to_variable = { USA_BONUS_urban_rep_val = .01 }
			custom_effect_tooltip = USA_urban_rep_shift
			custom_effect_tooltip = USA_bonus_tooltip

			set_temp_variable = { USA_week_change_urban_domestic_policy_con = 4 }
			add_to_variable = { Policy_Shift_urban_domestic_policy_con_Weeks = USA_week_change_urban_domestic_policy_con }
			custom_effect_tooltip = USA_urban_domestic_policy_con
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					var = USA_crime_bill_harsh
					value = 0.50
					compare = less_than
				}
				check_variable = {
					var = USA_crime_bill_harsh
					value = 0.30
					compare = greater_than
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = USA_fair_cb

			custom_effect_tooltip = USA_urban_voters_header_tt
			set_temp_variable = { USA_week_change_urban_dem = 2 }
			add_to_variable = { Demographic_Shift_urban_dem_Weeks = USA_week_change_urban_dem }
			add_to_variable = { USA_BONUS_urban_dem_val = .01 }
			custom_effect_tooltip = USA_urban_dem_shift
			custom_effect_tooltip = USA_bonus_tooltip
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					var = USA_crime_bill_harsh
					value = 0.75
					compare = less_than
				}
				check_variable = {
					var = USA_crime_bill_harsh
					value = 0.50
					compare = greater_than
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = USA_harsh_cb


			custom_effect_tooltip = USA_urban_voters_header_tt
			set_temp_variable = { USA_week_change_urban_dem = 3 }
			add_to_variable = { Demographic_Shift_urban_dem_Weeks = USA_week_change_urban_dem }
			add_to_variable = { USA_BONUS_urban_dem_val = .02 }
			custom_effect_tooltip = USA_urban_dem_shift
			custom_effect_tooltip = USA_bonus_tooltip
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					var = USA_crime_bill_harsh
					value = 0.75
					compare = greater_than
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = USA_very_harsh_cb

			custom_effect_tooltip = USA_urban_voters_header_tt
			set_temp_variable = { USA_week_change_urban_dem = 2 }
			add_to_variable = { Demographic_Shift_urban_dem_Weeks = USA_week_change_urban_dem }
			add_to_variable = { USA_BONUS_urban_dem_val = .01 }
			custom_effect_tooltip = USA_urban_dem_shift
			custom_effect_tooltip = USA_bonus_tooltip

			set_temp_variable = { USA_week_change_urban_domestic_policy_lib = 4 }
			add_to_variable = { Policy_Shift_urban_domestic_policy_lib_Weeks = USA_week_change_urban_domestic_policy_lib }
			custom_effect_tooltip = USA_urban_domestic_policy_lib

			hidden_effect = {
				# crime wave
				country_event = {
					id = hart.crimewave.1
					days = 90
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Hart helps kennedy prepare for a speech about health care
	id = hart.kennedy.3
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event hart.kennedy.3"
	hidden_effect = {
			#Cancel ANY current bill and prevent future bills from appearing
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = bill_enable_mission_hart
				}
				clr_country_flag = bill_enable_mission_hart
				clr_country_flag = USA_land_reform_act
				clr_country_flag = USA_americas_choice_act
				clr_country_flag = USA_responsibility_in_government_act
				clr_country_flag = USA_workers_wekfare_act
				clr_country_flag = USA_transport_ass_act
				clr_country_flag = USA_federal_finance_act
				clr_country_flag = USA_urban_divose_act
				clr_country_flag = USA_libraries_act
				clr_country_flag = USA_urban_affairs
				clr_country_flag = USA_bad_bayh
				clr_country_flag = USA_good_bayh
				clr_country_flag = USA_ted_kennedy_healthcare_bill
				clr_country_flag = USA_walter_reuther_pollution
				clr_country_flag = USA_kissinger_pakt_embargo
				clr_country_flag = USA_kissinger_popular_treaty
				clr_country_flag = USA_kissinger_unpopular_treaty
				clr_country_flag = USA_kissinger_PAST
			}
			set_country_flag = USA_chain_bill
		}
	}
	title = hart.kennedy.3.t
	desc = hart.kennedy.3.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_ted_kennedy_healthcare

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = hart.kennedy.3.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_ted_kennedy_health_insurrance_bill_tt
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = bill_enable_mission_hart
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = USA_hart_bill_cancelled_due_to_event_tt
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			national_health_insurrance = yes
			set_country_flag = USA_ted_kennedy_healthcare_bill
			set_country_flag = bill_enable_mission_hart
			set_variable = { USA_bill_mission_deadline_hart = 13 }
			activate_mission = USA_Hart_Bill_Countdown
		}
	}
}

				custom_effect_tooltip = USA_birch_bayh_bill_tt
				hidden_effect = {
					USA_Bayh_VP_Fail = yes

					set_country_flag = bill_enable_mission_hart
					set_variable = { USA_bill_mission_deadline_hart = 7 }
					activate_mission = USA_Hart_Bill_Countdown

				}
			}
		}

	desc = kirk.12.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_kirk_pin

	trigger = { # MCS or Harrington are not President
		OR = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = USA_68_FR_NPP
				has_country_flag = USA_68_C_NPP
			}
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = kirk.12.a

	}
}
